     <h1 class="post-title mob-marg-b-25 med-marg-b-50 big-marg-b-50" data-js="postTitle" itemprop="name" tabindex="0">
      5 Maps That Could Help Solve Some of the Worlds Most Daunting Problems
     </h1>
    </header>
    <section class="post-container clearfix relative" data-js="post" id="start-of-content" tabindex="0">
     <article class="content link-underline relative body-copy" data-js="content" itemprop="articleBody">
      <div id="container">
       <div class="row margin-top padding-top-extra">
        <p class="small-quotes no-margin padding-bottom">
         Slum Infrastructure: A Locals Guide To Kibera
        </p>
       </div>
       <div class="row">
        <div class="magnify-wrapper lazy-load-off">
         <img class="zoom-img" height="441" id="kibera-map" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/kibera_small.jpg" width="660"/>
         <div class="zoom-box" id="kibera-map-zoom">
          <img height="1068" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/kibera_large.gif" width="1600"/>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="row mobify-hide">
        <img class="no-margin col-8 padding-bottom" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/11/ff_maps_kiberakey_f.png"/>
       </div>
       <div class="row padding-top">
        <p>
         African maps are notoriously problematic. Much of the data is old; roads, particularly footpaths, languish unnamed. Africans often navigate by informal landmarks like bars or gas stations, places not represented on standard maps. The slums have it even worse: On Google Maps they figure as blank expanses, in keeping with their reputation as shadowy, marginal places.
        </p>
        <p>
         Enter Spatial Collective and Map Kibera. These two organizations, a company and a nonprofit, are mapping a Kenyan mega-slum called Kiberathe name is derived from a word meaning jungleaccording to how its 200,000 inhabitants actually navigate it. The maps started with crowdsourced landmarks important to locals: water taps, schools, pharmacies. Residents with Internet access were invited to add to an open source map; others contributed data by SMS or attended community workshops, where they wrote on giant empty maps.
        </p>
        <p>
         Spatial Collective overlays these community-generated maps with official data. One project tacked on sewer-line data (depicted here) from Nairobi City Water to find the most valuable spots to build new public toilets. Another mapped community-reported crime data to help the World Bank understand where to place safety interventions like lamps. These kinds of projects make Kibera more legible to its inhabitants
         <em>
          and
         </em>
         to outsiders.
        </p>
        <p class="uppercase brandon small no-margin">
         By Eve Fairbanks
         <span class="caption mobify-hide padding-bottom">
          <img class="ill-icon" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/10/illustration_icon.jpg"/>
          John Grimwade
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

       <script>
        (function(){
jQuery(document).ready(function () {
jQuery('.wide-post .social-top,.wide-post .entry-header').appendTo("#header");
jQuery('.wide-post .left_column,.wide-post .right_column').wrapAll("&lt;div class='footer_columns'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");

	// Popup boxes
		jQuery( "a.popup-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeIn();
			}
		});
           

                 //magnify hover
                 jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).hover(
			function(e){
                                return;
			},
			function(e){
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom").hide();
			}
		);

		jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).mousemove(
			function(e){
				var parentOffset = jQuery(this).parent().offset();
				var offX = e.clientX - parentOffset.left + jQuery(window).scrollLeft(),
					offY = e.clientY - parentOffset.top + jQuery(window).scrollTop();
				offsetMap(jQuery(this), jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom"), offX, offY);
			}
		);

		function offsetMap(small, big, x, y) {
			// Limit X and Y for edges
			big.show();
			var boxW = big.width(),
				boxH = big.height(),
				boxWh = boxW / 2,
				boxHh = boxH / 2,
				smallW = small.width(),
				smallH = small.height();
			// Map X and Y from small image onto big
			var bigW = big.find("img").width();
			big.hide();


			var ratio = bigW / smallW;
			var bigX = x * ratio,
			      bigY = y * ratio;
			big.find("img").css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: -bigX + boxWh,
				top: -bigY + boxHh
			});
			big.css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: x - boxWh,
				top: y - boxHh,
			});
                }

		// Jakarta Map layers
		jQuery( "a.layer-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeIn();
			}
		});

       <div class="row mobify-hide">
        <img class="padding-top-bottom col-6" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/11/maps_carbonkey2.jpg"/>
       </div>
       <div class="row padding-top">
        <p>
         The stuff that causes global climate changecarbon dioxide, methane, and other greenhouse gasesdoesnt spread out in a homogenous vapor. It accumulates in domes and plumes, mostly above cities. Levels ebb and flow with time of day and season, varying not just from city to city but neighborhood to neighborhood. The Megacities Carbon Project aims to understand that flow with exactitude. The map here shows a model of data from Indianapolis; Los Angeles, Boston, Salt Lake City, and Paris are carrying out similar projects.
        </p>
        <p>
         In LA, where a ring of mountains traps carbon as well as it does smog, that will mean installing 16 ground-based spectrometers (around a dozen are up so far). Soon theyll also get data from the Orbiting Carbon Observatory, a satellite scheduled to launch in summer 2014. Cities are very complex. Thats why you need a lot of stations and very dense observation, says Riley Duren, a NASA Jet Propulsion Lab engineer working on the project. Some places dont emit at all, and some places look like a hot spot.
        </p>
        <p>
         The point of mapping carbon at such high resolution? Were trying to link cause and effect, Duren says. Sensors could help catch factories flouting emissions laws or identify unexpected carbon culprits. If nations wont make progress on climate, perhaps cities will.
        </p>
        <p class="uppercase brandon small no-margin">
         By Adam Rogers
         <span class="caption mobify-hide padding-bottom">
          <img class="ill-icon" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/10/illustration_icon.jpg"/>
          CleverFranke
         </span>
        </p>
        <p class="caption">
         Source: Kevin Gurney, Arizona State University
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeIn();

                 jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).hover(
			function(e){
                                return;
			},
			function(e){
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom").hide();
			}
		);

		jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).mousemove(
			function(e){
				var parentOffset = jQuery(this).parent().offset();
				var offX = e.clientX - parentOffset.left + jQuery(window).scrollLeft(),
					offY = e.clientY - parentOffset.top + jQuery(window).scrollTop();
				offsetMap(jQuery(this), jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom"), offX, offY);
			}
		);

		function offsetMap(small, big, x, y) {
			// Limit X and Y for edges
			big.show();
			var boxW = big.width(),
				boxH = big.height(),
				boxWh = boxW / 2,
				boxHh = boxH / 2,
				smallW = small.width(),
				smallH = small.height();
			// Map X and Y from small image onto big
			var bigW = big.find("img").width();
			big.hide();


			var ratio = bigW / smallW;
			var bigX = x * ratio,
			      bigY = y * ratio;
			big.find("img").css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: -bigX + boxWh,
				top: -bigY + boxHh
			});
			big.css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: x - boxWh,
				top: y - boxHh,
			});
                }

		// Jakarta Map layers
		jQuery( "a.layer-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();

				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeIn();
			}
		});

      <div id="container">
       <div class="row margin-top padding-top-extra">
        <p class="small-quotes padding-bottom no-margin">
         Development: Financial Services in Nigeria
        </p>
       </div>
       <div class="row">
        <div class="magnify-wrapper lazy-load-off">
         <img class="zoom-img" height="536" id="kibera-map" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/nigeria_small.jpg" width="660"/>
         <div class="zoom-box" id="kibera-map-zoom">
          <img height="1137" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/nigeria_large2.gif" width="1400"/>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="row mobify-hide">
        <img class="no-margin padding-bottom" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/11/ff_maps_financialkey.png"/>
       </div>
       <div class="row padding-top">
        <p>
         Before households can rise out of poverty, they need access to financial tools: the basic banking, payment, credit, and insurance services that Westerners take for granted. So in January, the Gates Foundations Financial Services for the Poor program launched an ambitious geospatial project in Nigeria. Armed with BlackBerrys and traveling in a grid pattern, 30 surveyors undertook a three-month campaign in Nigeria to pinpoint all of the services availablefrom bank branches to microfinance institutions to post offices and more. They logged GPS coordinates and took photos. (The program had to rescue one surveyor from the police after he aroused suspicion at a bank.)
        </p>
        <p>
         The resulting website gives the best picture yet of how financial services work in a developing economy. Jake Kendall, the Gates Foundation program officer who heads the project, hopes financial institutions will use the map to figure out where to open new locations. It can also guide public policy: Kendalls team used this map to show the Nigerian central bank governor the need for mobile-based financial services, since it demonstrates that more than half of residents live outside a 3-mile radius of brick-and-mortar options. Besides Nigeria, the Gates team has already mapped Tanzania, Uganda, Kenya, and Bangladesh, with India and Indonesia coming soon.
        </p>
        <p class="uppercase brandon small no-margin">
         By Victoria Tang
         <span class="caption mobify-hide padding-bottom">
          <img class="ill-icon" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/10/illustration_icon.jpg"/>
          John Grimwade
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

jQuery(document).ready(function () {
jQuery('.wide-post .social-top,.wide-post .entry-header').appendTo("#header");
jQuery('.wide-post .left_column,.wide-post .right_column').wrapAll("&lt;div class='footer_columns'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");

	// Popup boxes
		jQuery( "a.popup-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeIn();
			}
		});
           

                 //magnify hover
                 jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).hover(
			function(e){
                                return;
			},
			function(e){
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom").hide();
			}
		);

		jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).mousemove(
			function(e){
				var parentOffset = jQuery(this).parent().offset();
				var offX = e.clientX - parentOffset.left + jQuery(window).scrollLeft(),
					offY = e.clientY - parentOffset.top + jQuery(window).scrollTop();
				offsetMap(jQuery(this), jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom"), offX, offY);
			}
		);

		function offsetMap(small, big, x, y) {
			// Limit X and Y for edges
			big.show();
			var boxW = big.width(),
				boxH = big.height(),
				boxWh = boxW / 2,
				boxHh = boxH / 2,
				smallW = small.width(),
				smallH = small.height();
			// Map X and Y from small image onto big
			var bigW = big.find("img").width();
			big.hide();


			var ratio = bigW / smallW;
			var bigX = x * ratio,
			      bigY = y * ratio;
			big.find("img").css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: -bigX + boxWh,
				top: -bigY + boxHh
			});
			big.css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: x - boxWh,
				top: y - boxHh,
			});
                }

		// Jakarta Map layers
		jQuery( "a.layer-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeIn();
			}
		});

jQuery( "#slider" ).slider({
			min: 1,
			max: 24,

      <div id="container">
       <div class="row margin-top padding-top-extra">
        <p class="small-quotes padding-bottom no-margin">
         Health: US Medical Readmission
        </p>
       </div>
       <div class="row mobify-hide">
        <a href="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/healthcare_map_large2.jpg">
         <img src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/healthcare_map_large2.jpg"/>
        </a>
        <p>
         <img class="col-8 padding-top-bottom no-margin" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/11/ff_maps_medicalkey_f.png"/>
        </p>
       </div>
       <div class="row padding-top">
        <p>
         For more than 20 years, the Dartmouth Atlas of Health Care has been producing uncomfortable revelations about the US health care system. For example, regions that spend the most money dont necessarily provide the best care. And doctors with access to fancy scanners and expensive diagnostic tests are more likely to use them, whether patients need them or not. By mining and mapping data on Medicare in particular, Dartmouth researchers have shown that the quality and efficiency of medical care varies surprisingly from place to place; the White House and Congress discussed these findings often in their recent debates over health care reform.
        </p>
        <p>
         This map shows one of the Dartmouth teams newer discoveries. Red crosses indicate regions where more patients wind up in the emergency room within 30 days of being discharged from the hospital. This is especially disturbing when patients suffer from heart disease or other chronic illnesses that require long-term care. Ideally, hospitals help coordinate continued treatment with the patients primary care physicians after theyre discharged. But in many places that doesnt happen, says David Goodman, codirector of the atlas, because too many administrators believe their responsibility ends at the hospital door.
        </p>
        <p class="uppercase brandon small no-margin">
         By Greg Miller
         <span class="caption mobify-hide padding-bottom">
          <img class="ill-icon" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/10/illustration_icon.jpg"/>
          CleverFranke
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

       <script>
        (function(){
jQuery(document).ready(function () {
jQuery('.wide-post .social-top,.wide-post .entry-header').appendTo("#header");
jQuery('.wide-post .left_column,.wide-post .right_column').wrapAll("&lt;div class='footer_columns'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");

	// Popup boxes
		jQuery( "a.popup-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeIn();
			}
		});
           

                 //magnify hover
                 jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).hover(
			function(e){
                                return;
			},
			function(e){
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom").hide();
			}
		);

		jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).mousemove(
			function(e){
				var parentOffset = jQuery(this).parent().offset();
				var offX = e.clientX - parentOffset.left + jQuery(window).scrollLeft(),
					offY = e.clientY - parentOffset.top + jQuery(window).scrollTop();
				offsetMap(jQuery(this), jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom"), offX, offY);
			}
		);

		function offsetMap(small, big, x, y) {
			// Limit X and Y for edges
			big.show();
			var boxW = big.width(),
				boxH = big.height(),
				boxWh = boxW / 2,
				boxHh = boxH / 2,
				smallW = small.width(),
				smallH = small.height();
			// Map X and Y from small image onto big
			var bigW = big.find("img").width();
			big.hide();


			var ratio = bigW / smallW;
			var bigX = x * ratio,
			      bigY = y * ratio;
			big.find("img").css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: -bigX + boxWh,
				top: -bigY + boxHh
			});
			big.css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: x - boxWh,
				top: y - boxHh,
			});
                }

		// Jakarta Map layers
		jQuery( "a.layer-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeIn();
			}
		});

       <div class="row padding-top">
        <p>
         Jakarta is sinking. Two-fifths of the Indonesian capital sits below sea level, and the lowest areas are also the least mapped. Surrounded by a labyrinth of flood-prone waterways, residents must always brace for the worst.
        </p>
        <p>
         But before this years deluges (the rainy season begins in November and lasts until June), a new planning tool came online. More than 250 village lurahs, or leaders, received maps of the critical infrastructure in their communities: schools, municipal buildings, hospitals, mosques, and more. In addition, areas inundated by recent floods were clearly marked.
        </p>
        <p>
         The maps were made possible by a nonprofit called Humanitarian OpenStreetMap Team. HOT recruited geography undergrads from the University of Indonesia in 2012 to collect data. The students then held a series of workshops, teaching lurahs how to fill in a base map of their communities with landmarks. Altogether, they mapped 6,000 buildings. Now Indonesias National Disaster Management Agency is integrating this data with a free software plug-in called InaSAFE, which creates impact scenarios of future hazards. When the next flood rushes in, Jakartans will have better contingency plans in place.
        </p>
        <p class="uppercase brandon small no-margin">
         By Cameron Bird
         <span class="caption mobify-hide padding-bottom">
          <img class="ill-icon" src="http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2013/10/illustration_icon.jpg"/>
          John Grimwade
         </span>
        </p>
       </div>

t,i,s,a,n,r=this.options.range,o=this.options,h=this,l=this._animateOff?!1:o.animate,u={};this.options.values&amp;&amp;this.options.values.length?this.handles.each(function(s){i=100*((h.values(s)-h._valueMin())/(h._valueMax()-h._valueMin())),u["horizontal"===h.orientation?"left":"bottom"]=i+"%",e(this).stop(1,1)[l?"animate":"css"](u,o.animate),h.options.range===!0&amp;&amp;("horizontal"===h.orientation?(0===s&amp;&amp;h.range.stop(1,1)[l?"animate":"css"]({left:i+"%"},o.animate),1===s&amp;&amp;h.range[l?"animate":"css"]({width:i-t+"%"},{queue:!1,duration:o.animate})):(0===s&amp;&amp;h.range.stop(1,1)[l?"animate":"css"]({bottom:i+"%"},o.animate),1===s&amp;&amp;h.range[l?"animate":"css"]({height:i-t+"%"},{queue:!1,duration:o.animate}))),t=i}):(s=this.value(),a=this._valueMin(),n=this._valueMax(),i=n!==a?100*((s-a)/(n-a)):0,u["horizontal"===this.orientation?"left":"bottom"]=i+"%",this.handle.stop(1,1)[l?"animate":"css"](u,o.animate),"min"===r&amp;&amp;"horizontal"===this.orientation&amp;&amp;this.range.stop(1,1)[l?"animate":"css"]({width:i+"%"},o.animate),"max"===r&amp;&amp;"horizontal"===this.orientation&amp;&amp;this.range[l?"animate":"css"]({width:100-i+"%"},{queue:!1,duration:o.animate}),"min"===r&amp;&amp;"vertical"===this.orientation&amp;&amp;this.range.stop(1,1)[l?"animate":"css"]({height:i+"%"},o.animate),"max"===r&amp;&amp;"vertical"===this.orientation&amp;&amp;this.range[l?"animate":"css"]({height:100-i+"%"},{queue:!1,duration:o.animate}))},_handleEvents:{keydown:function(i){var s,a,n,r,o=e(i.target).data("ui-slider-handle-index");switch(i.keyCode){case e.ui.keyCode.HOME:case e.ui.keyCode.END:case e.ui.keyCode.PAGE_UP:case e.ui.keyCode.PAGE_DOWN:case e.ui.keyCode.UP:case e.ui.keyCode.RIGHT:case e.ui.keyCode.DOWN:case e.ui.keyCode.LEFT:if(i.preventDefault(),!this._keySliding&amp;&amp;(this._keySliding=!0,e(i.target).addClass("ui-state-active"),s=this._start(i,o),s===!1))return}switch(r=this.options.step,a=n=this.options.values&amp;&amp;this.options.values.length?this.values(o):this.value(),i.keyCode){case e.ui.keyCode.HOME:n=this._valueMin();break;case e.ui.keyCode.END:n=this._valueMax();break;case e.ui.keyCode.PAGE_UP:n=this._trimAlignValue(a+(this._valueMax()-this._valueMin())/t);break;case e.ui.keyCode.PAGE_DOWN:n=this._trimAlignValue(a-(this._valueMax()-this._valueMin())/t);break;case e.ui.keyCode.UP:case e.ui.keyCode.RIGHT:if(a===this._valueMax())return;n=this._trimAlignValue(a+r);break;case e.ui.keyCode.DOWN:case e.ui.keyCode.LEFT:if(a===this._valueMin())return;n=this._trimAlignValue(a-r)}this._slide(i,o,n)},click:function(e){e.preventDefault()},keyup:function(t){var i=e(t.target).data("ui-slider-handle-index");this._keySliding&amp;&amp;(this._keySliding=!1,this._stop(t,i),this._change(t,i),e(t.target).removeClass("ui-state-active"))}}})})(jQuery);
        </script>

        <script>
         (function(){
jQuery(document).ready(function () {
jQuery('.wide-post .social-top,.wide-post .entry-header').appendTo("#header");
jQuery('.wide-post .left_column,.wide-post .right_column').wrapAll("&lt;div class='footer_columns'&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");

	// Popup boxes
		jQuery( "a.popup-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery(".popup-box").fadeIn();
			}
		});
           

                 //magnify hover
                 jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).hover(
			function(e){
                                return;
			},
			function(e){
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom").hide();
			}
		);

		jQuery( ".zoom-img" ).mousemove(
			function(e){
				var parentOffset = jQuery(this).parent().offset();
				var offX = e.clientX - parentOffset.left + jQuery(window).scrollLeft(),
					offY = e.clientY - parentOffset.top + jQuery(window).scrollTop();
				offsetMap(jQuery(this), jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr('id') + "-zoom"), offX, offY);
			}
		);

		function offsetMap(small, big, x, y) {
			// Limit X and Y for edges
			big.show();
			var boxW = big.width(),
				boxH = big.height(),
				boxWh = boxW / 2,
				boxHh = boxH / 2,
				smallW = small.width(),
				smallH = small.height();
			// Map X and Y from small image onto big
			var bigW = big.find("img").width();
			big.hide();


			var ratio = bigW / smallW;
			var bigX = x * ratio,
			      bigY = y * ratio;
			big.find("img").css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: -bigX + boxWh,
				top: -bigY + boxHh
			});
			big.css({
                                display: 'block',
				left: x - boxWh,
				top: y - boxHh,
			});
                }

		// Jakarta Map layers
		jQuery( "a.layer-btn" ).click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			jQuery(this).toggleClass("active");
			if (!jQuery(this).is(".active")) {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeOut();
			} else {
				jQuery("#" + jQuery(this).attr("id") + "-map").fadeIn();
			}
		});

//carbon map
if(jQuery("#slider").length) {
        var imgs = [
		"http://www.wired.com/images_blogs/wiredscience/2015/11/carbon_hour_001.jpg",

	for (i in imgs) {

	}
}
jQuery( "#slider" ).slider({
			min: 1,
			max: 24,
			slide: function( event, ui ) {

            function generateId(url) {
                var urlRegexp;
                if (url.indexOf("https:") === 0) {
                    urlRegexp = /https:\/\/[^\/]*\/([^?#]*).*/i;
                } else {
                    urlRegexp = /http:\/\/[^\/]*\/([^?#]*).*/i;
                }
                url.match(urlRegexp);
                return RegExp.$1;
            }
